Hello, I'm Ad Taylor.

I am a web designer and founder of Meta Union, a small web design and development shop based in Birmingham, UK.

You can see some of my work on Dribbble or on Github. I can also be found on Twitter, Flickr and Instagram. Or send me an e-mail, if that's your thing.
